self.offset = offset;\n    54→        self.clampOffset();\n    55→    }\n    56→\n    57→    /// Scroll by a delta amount (positive = down, negative = up).\n    58→    pub fn scrollBy(self: *ScrollState, delta: i32) void {\n    59→        if (delta < 0) {\n    60→            const abs_delta: usize = @intCast(-delta);\n    61→            self.offset -|= abs_delta;\n    62→        } else /// Scroll up by one line.\n    70→    pub fn scrollUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n    71→        self.scrollBy(-1);\n    72→    }\n    73→\n    74→    /// Scroll down by one line.\n    75→    pub fn void {\n    81→        self.scrollBy(-@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    82→    }\n    83→\n    84→    /// Scroll down by one page (viewport height).\n    85→    pub fn pageDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n    86→        self.scrollBy(@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    87→    }\n    88→\n    89→    /// Scroll to the beginning.\n    90→    pub fn scrollToStart(self: *ScrollState) void {\n    91→        self.offset = 0;\n    92→    }\n    93→\n    94→    /// Scroll to the end.\n    95→    pub fn scrollToEnd(self: *ScrollState) void {\n    96→        self.offset =       if (index < self.offset) {\n   102→            self.offset = index;\n   103→        } else if (index >= self.offset + self.viewport) {\n   104→            self.offset = index -| (self.viewport -| 1);\n   105→        }\n   106→        self.clampOffset();\n   107→    }\n   108→\n   109→    /// Get the maximum valid scroll offset.\n   110→    pub fn maxOffset(self: ScrollState) usize {\n   111→        if (self.total <= self.viewport) return 0;\n   112→        return self.total - self.viewport;\n   113→    }\n   114→\n   115→    /// Check if currently at the top.\n   116→    pub fn atStart(self: ScrollState) bool {\n   117→        return self.offset == 0;\n   118→    }\n   119→\n   120→    /// Check if currently at the bottom.\n   121→    pub fn atEnd(self: ScrollState) bool {\n key: Key) bool {\n   145→        switch (key.code) {\n   146→            .up => {\n   147→                self.scrollUp();\n   148→                return true;\n   149→            },\n   150→             return true;\n   157→            },\n   158→            .page_down => {\n   159→                self.pageDown();\n   160→                return true;\n   161→            },\n   162→            .home => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n   163→                self.scrollToStart();\n   164→                return true;\n   165→            },\n   166→            .end => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n   167→                self.scrollToEnd();\n   168→                return true;\n   169→            },\n   170→            else => {},\n   171→        }\n   172→        return false;\n   173→    }\n   174→\n   175→    /// Handle mouse scroll events.\n   176→    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n   177→    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n   178→        switch                self.scrollBy(3);\n   185→                return true;\n   186→            },\n   187→            else => {},\n   188→        }\n   189→        return false;\n   190→    }\n   191→};\n /// Get the content area (viewport minus scrollbar if shown).\n   215→    pub fn contentArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n   216→        if (!self.show_scrollbar or !self.state.canScroll()) {\n   217→            return area;\n   218→        }\n   219→\n   220→        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n   221→            return Rect.init(\n   222→                area.x +| 1,\n   223→                area.y,\n   224→                area.width -| 1,\n   225→                area.height,\n   226→            );\n   227→        } else {\n   228→            return Rect.init(\n   229→                area.x,\n   230→                area.y,\n   231→                area.width -| 1,\n   232→                area.height,\n   233→            );\n   234→        }\n   235→    }\n   236→\n   237→    /// Get the scrollbar area.\n   238→    pub fn scrollbarArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n   239→        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n   240→            return Rect.init(area.x, area.y, 1, area.height);\n   241→        } else {\n   242→            return Rect.init(area.x +| (area.width -| 1), area.y, 1, area.height);\n   243→        }\n   244→    }\n   245→\n   246→    /// Render the scrollbar (if needed).\n   247→    pub fn render(self: ScrollView, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   248→        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   249→\n   250→        // Update viewport in scroll state\n   251→        self.state.setViewport(area.height);\n   252→\n   253→        // Fill background\n   254→        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n   255→            buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n   256→        }\n   257→\n   258→        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n   259→        if (self.show_scrollbar and self.state.canScroll()) {\n   260→            const sb_area = self.scrollbarArea(area);\n   261→            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n   262→                .total = self.state.total,\n   263→                .position = self.state.offset,\n   264→                .viewport = self.state.viewport,\n   265→                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n   266→                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n   267→                .orientation = .vertical,\n   268→            };\n   269→            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n   270→        }\n   271→    }\n   272→};\n   273→\n   274→/// ScrollableList combines List behavior with virtual scrolling.\n   275→/// Renders only visible items and integrates with ScrollState.\n   276→pub const ScrollableList = struct {\n   277→    /// Items to display.\n   278→    items: []const []const u8,\n   279→\n   280→    /// Scroll state.\n   281→    scroll: *ScrollState,\n   282→\n   283→    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection).\n   284→    selected: ?usize = null,\n   285→\n   286→    /// Default style for non-selected items.\n   287→    style: Style = Style.empty,\n   288→\n   289→    /// Style for the selected item.\n   290→    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n   291→\n   292→    /// Prefix shown before the selected item.\n   293→    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n   294→\n   295→    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n   296→    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n   297→\n   298→    /// Scrollbar style.\n   299→    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n   300→\n   301→    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n   302→    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n   303→\n   304→    /// Update scroll state from items.\n   305→    pub fn syncState(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   306→        self.scroll.setTotal(self.items.len);\n   307→        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   308→            self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel);\n   309→        }\n   310→    }\n   311→\n   312→    /// Move selection up.\n   313→    pub fn selectPrevious(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   314→        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   315→        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   316→            if (sel > 0) {\n   317→                self.selected = sel - 1;\n   318→                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel - 1);\n   319→            }\n   320→        } else {\n   321→            self.selected = 0;\n   322→            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   323→        }\n   324→    }\n   325→\n   326→    /// Move selection down.\n   327→    pub fn selectNext(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   328→        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   329→        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   330→            if (sel + 1 < self.items.len) {\n   331→                self.selected = sel + 1;\n   332→                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel + 1);\n   333→            }\n   334→        } else {\n   335→            self.selected = 0;\n   336→            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   337→        }\n   338→    }\n   339→\n   340→    /// Select first item.\n   341→    pub fn selectFirst(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   342→        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   343→        self.selected = 0;\n   344→        self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   345→    }\n   346→\n   347→    /// Select last item.\n   348→    pub fn selectLast(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   349→        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   350→        self.selected = self.items.len - 1;\n   351→        self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.items.len - 1);\n   352→    }\n   353→\n   354→    /// Handle keyboard input for navigation.\n   355→    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n   356→    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollableList, key: Key) bool {\n   357→        switch (key.code) {\n   358→            .up => {\n   359→                self.selectPrevious();\n   360→                return true;\n   361→            },\n   362→            .down => {\n   363→                self.selectNext();\n   364→                return true;\n   365→            },\n   366→            .home => {\n   367→                self.selectFirst();\n   368→                return true;\n   369→            },\n   370→            .end => {\n   371→                self.selectLast();\n   372→                return true;\n   373→            },\n   374→            .page_up => {\n   375→                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n   376→                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   377→                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n   378→                    self.selected = sel -| page;\n   379→                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n   380→                }\n   381→                return true;\n   382→            },\n   383→            .page_down => {\n   384→                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n   385→                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   386→                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n   387→                    self.selected = @min(sel + page, self.items.len -| 1);\n   388→                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n   389→                }\n   390→                return true;\n   391→            },\n   392→            else => {},\n   393→        }\n   394→        return false;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    /// Render the scrollable list.\n   398→    pub fn render(self: ScrollableList, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   399→        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   400→\n   401→        // Calculate content area (minus scrollbar if needed)\n   402→        const needs_scrollbar = self.show_scrollbar and self.items.len > area.height;\n   403→        const content_width = if (needs_scrollbar) area.width -| 1 else area.width;\n   404→        const content_area = Rect.init(area.x, area.y, content_width, area.height);\n   405→\n   406→        if (content_area.isEmpty()) return;\n   407→\n   408→        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, content_area.width));\n   409→        const content_start = content_area.x +| symbol_len;\n   410→        const text_width = content_area.width -| symbol_len;\n   411→\n   412→        // Get visible range\n   413→        const range = self.scroll.visibleRange();\n   414→\n   415→        // Render visible items\n   416→        var y = content_area.y;\n   417→        var item_index = range.start;\n   418→        while (item_index < range.end and y < content_area.bottom()) : ({\n   419→            y += 1;\n   420→            item_index += 1;\n   421→        }) {\n   422→            const item = self.items[item_index];\n   423→            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n   424→\n   425→            if (is_selected) {\n   426→                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n   427→                const row_rect = Rect.init(content_area.x, y, content_area.width, 1);\n   428→                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n   429→\n   430→                // Draw highlight symbol\n   431→                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n   432→                    buf.setString(content_area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n   433→                }\n   434→\n   435→                // Draw item text with highlight style\n   436→                if (text_width > 0) {\n   437→                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n   438→                }\n   439→            } else {\n   440→                // Draw item text with normal style\n   441→                if (text_width > 0) {\n   442→                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n   443→                }\n   444→            }\n   445→        }\n   446→\n   447→        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n   448→        if (needs_scrollbar) {\n   449→            const sb_area = Rect.init(area.x +| content_width, area.y, 1, area.height);\n   450→            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n   451→                .total = self.items.len,\n   452→                .position = self.scroll.offset,\n   453→                .viewport = area.height,\n   454→                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n   455→                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n   456→                .orientation = .vertical,\n   457→            };\n   458→            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n   459→        }\n   460→    }\n   461→\n   462→    /// Get the number of items.\n   463→    pub fn len(self: ScrollableList) usize {\n   464→        return self.items.len;\n   465→    }\n   466→\n   467→    /// Check if empty.\n   468→    pub fn isEmpty(self: ScrollableList) bool {\n   469→        return self.items.len == 0;\n   470→    }\n   471→};\n   472→\n   473→// ============================================================\n   474→// SANITY TESTS - ScrollState basic functionality\n   475→// ============================================================\n   476→\n   477→test \"sanity: ScrollState default values\" {\n   478→    const state = ScrollState{};\n   479→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n   480→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.total);\n   481→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), state.viewport);\n   482→}\n   483→\n   484→test \"sanity: ScrollState.init\" {\n   485→    const state = ScrollState.init(100);\n   486→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n   487→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), state.total);\n   488→}\n   489→\n   490→test \"sanity: ScrollState.setViewport\" {\n   491→    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n   492→    state.setViewport(20);\n   493→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), state.viewport);\n   494→}\n   495→\n   496→test \"sanity: ScrollState.maxOffset\" {\n   497→    var state = {\n   503→    var small = ScrollState.init(10);\n   504→    small.setViewport(20);\n   505→    try std.testing.expect(!small.canScroll());\n   506→\n   507→    var large = ScrollState.init(100);\n   508→    large.setViewport(20);\n   509→    try std.testing.expect(large.canScroll());\n   510→}\n   511→\n   512→// ============================================================\n   513→// BEHAVIOR state.scrollTo(90);\n   524→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n   525→\n   526→    state.scrollTo(0);\n   527→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n   539→\n   540→    state.scrollBy(-100);\n   541→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n   542→\n   543→    state.scrollBy(200);\n   544→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n   545→}\n   546→\n   547→test \"behavior: ScrollState.pageUp and pageDown\" {\n   548→    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n   549→    state.setViewport(20);\n   550→\n   551→    state.scrollTo(50);\n   552→    state.pageUp();\n   553→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 30), state.offset);\n   554→\n   555→    state.pageDown();\n   556→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n   557→}\n   558→\n   559→test \"behavior: ScrollState.scrollToStart and scrollToEnd\" {\n   560→    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n   561→    state.setViewport(20);\n   562→\n   563→    state.scrollTo(50);\n   564→    state.scrollToStart();\n   565→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n   566→    try std.testing.expect(state.atStart());\n   567→\n   568→    state.scrollToEnd();\n   569→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n   570→    try std.testing.expect(state.atEnd());\n   571→}\n   572→\n   573→test \"behavior: ScrollState.ensureVisible\" {\n   574→    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n   575→    state.setViewport(20);\n   576→    state.scrollTo(50);\n   577→\n   578→    // Item already visible\n   579→    state.ensureVisible(55);\n   580→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n   581→\n   582→    // Item above viewport\n   583→    state.ensureVisible(40);\n   584→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 40), state.offset);\n   585→\n   586→    // Item below viewport\n   587→    state.ensureVisible(80);\n   588→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 61), state.offset);\n   589→}\n   590→\n   591→test \"behavior: ScrollState.visibleRange\" {\n   592→    var state = std.testing.expect(handled_pgup);\n   626→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 30), state.offset);\n   627→\n   628→    const handled_pgdn = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .page_down });\n   629→    try std.testing.expect(handled_pgdn);\n   630→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n   631→}\n   632→\n   633→test \"behavior: ScrollState.handleMouse scroll\" {\n   634→    .items = &items,\n   695→        .scroll = &state,\n   696→    };\n   697→\n   698→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), list.len());\n   699→    try std.testing.expect(!list.isEmpty());\n   700→    try std.testing.expect(list.selected == null);\n   701→}\n   702→\n   703→test \"sanity: ScrollableList.syncState\" {\n   704→    var state = ScrollState{};\n   705→    const items = 720→test \"behavior: ScrollableList.selectPrevious and selectNext\" {\n   721→    var state = ScrollState{};\n   722→    state.setViewport(3);\n   723→    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", list.syncState();\n   730→\n   731→    list.selectNext();\n   732→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 3), list.selected);\n   733→\n   734→    list.selectPrevious();\n   735→    try state.setViewport(3);\n   741→    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\" };\n   742→    var list = ScrollableList{\n   743→        .items = &items,\n   744→        .scroll =   757→    var state = ScrollState{};\n   758→    state.setViewport(3);\n   759→    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\", \"f\", \"g\", \"h\" };\n   760→    var list = state.setViewport(3);\n   809→    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\", \"Delta\", \"Epsilon\" };\n   810→    var list = ScrollableList{\n   811→        .items = &items,\n [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\", \"Delta\", \"Epsilon\" };\n   833→    var list = ScrollableList{\n   834→        .items = &items,\n   835→        .scroll = &state,\n   836→  842→\n   843→    // Scrollbar should be in last column\n   844→    const sb_cell = buf.get(19, 0);\n   845→    try std.testing.expect(sb_cell.style.hasAttribute(.reverse));\n   846→}\n   847→\n   848→test \"behavior: ScrollableList renders selection\" {\n   849→    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n   850→    defer buf.deinit();\n   851→\n   852→    var state = ScrollState{};\n   853→    state.setViewport(3);\n   854→    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\" };\n   855→    var list = ScrollableList{\n   856→        .items = &items,\n ScrollView widget for zithril TUI framework\n// Virtual scrolling container with scroll state management and scrollbar integration\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\nconst scrollbar_mod = @import(\"scrollbar.zig\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"../event.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\npub const Scrollbar = scrollbar_mod.Scrollbar;\npub const Orientation = scrollbar_mod.Orientation;\npub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\npub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\npub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\npub const Key = event_mod.Key;\n\n/// Scroll state for a scrollable container.\n/// Tracks scroll position and provides helpers for navigation.\npub const ScrollState = struct {\n    /// Current vertical scroll offset (first visible row).\n    offset: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Total number of items/rows in the content.\n    total: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Viewport height (number of visible rows).\n    viewport: u16 = 0,\n\n    /// Create a new scroll state.\n    pub fn init(total: usize) ScrollState {\n        return .{ .total = total };\n    }\n\n    /// Update viewport size and clamp offset if needed.\n    pub fn setViewport(self: *ScrollState, viewport: u16) void {\n        self.viewport = viewport;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Update total content size and clamp offset if needed.\n    pub fn setTotal(self: *ScrollState, total: usize) void {\n        self.total = total;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to a specific offset (clamped to valid range).\n    pub fn scrollTo(self: *ScrollState, offset: usize) void {\n        self.offset = offset;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll by a delta amount (positive = down, negative = up).\n    pub fn scrollBy(self: *ScrollState, delta: i32) void {\n        if (delta < 0) {\n            const abs_delta: usize = @intCast(-delta);\n            self.offset -|= abs_delta;\n        } else {\n            const pos_delta: usize = @intCast(delta);\n            self.offset +|= pos_delta;\n        }\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll up by one line.\n    pub fn scrollUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(-1);\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll down by one line.\n    pub fn scrollDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(1);\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll up by one page (viewport height).\n    pub fn pageUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(-@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll down by one page (viewport height).\n    pub fn pageDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to the beginning.\n    pub fn scrollToStart(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to the end.\n    pub fn scrollToEnd(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = self.maxOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Ensure a specific index is visible, scrolling if necessary.\n    pub fn ensureVisible(self: *ScrollState, index: usize) void {\n        if (index < self.offset) {\n            self.offset = index;\n        } else if (index >= self.offset + self.viewport) {\n            self.offset = index -| (self.viewport -| 1);\n        }\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Get the maximum valid scroll offset.\n    pub fn maxOffset(self: ScrollState) usize {\n        if (self.total <= self.viewport) return 0;\n        return self.total - self.viewport;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if currently at the top.\n    pub fn atStart(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.offset == 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if currently at the bottom.\n    pub fn atEnd(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.offset >= self.maxOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Check if scrolling is needed (content exceeds viewport).\n    pub fn canScroll(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.total > self.viewport;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the range of visible indices [start, end).\n    pub fn visibleRange(self: ScrollState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n        const start = self.offset;\n        const end = @min(self.offset + self.viewport, self.total);\n        return .{ .start = start, .end = end };\n    }\n\n    /// Clamp offset to valid range.\n    fn clampOffset(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = @min(self.offset, self.maxOffset());\n    }\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input for scrolling.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollState, key: Key) bool {\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .up => {\n                self.scrollUp();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .down => {\n                self.scrollDown();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_up => {\n                self.pageUp();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_down => {\n                self.pageDown();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n                self.scrollToStart();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n                self.scrollToEnd();\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Handle mouse scroll events.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n        switch (mouse.kind) {\n            .scroll_up => {\n                self.scrollBy(-3);\n                return true;\n            },\n            .scroll_down => {\n                self.scrollBy(3);\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n};\n\n/// ScrollView widget configuration.\n/// Wraps content with virtual scrolling and optional scrollbar.\npub const ScrollView = struct {\n    /// Scroll state (tracks position).\n    state: *ScrollState,\n\n    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n\n    /// Scrollbar style.\n    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Background style for the viewport.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar position (right edge by default).\n    scrollbar_on_left: bool = false,\n\n    /// Get the content area (viewport minus scrollbar if shown).\n    pub fn contentArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n        if (!self.show_scrollbar or !self.state.canScroll()) {\n            return area;\n        }\n\n        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n            return Rect.init(\n                area.x +| 1,\n                area.y,\n                area.width -| 1,\n                area.height,\n            );\n        } else {\n            return Rect.init(\n                area.x,\n                area.y,\n                area.width -| 1,\n                area.height,\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the scrollbar area.\n    pub fn scrollbarArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n            return Rect.init(area.x, area.y, 1, area.height);\n        } else {\n            return Rect.init(area.x +| (area.width -| 1), area.y, 1, area.height);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Render the scrollbar (if needed).\n    pub fn render(self: ScrollView, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Update viewport in scroll state\n        self.state.setViewport(area.height);\n\n        // Fill background\n        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n            buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n        }\n\n        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n        if (self.show_scrollbar and self.state.canScroll()) {\n            const sb_area = self.scrollbarArea(area);\n            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n                .total = self.state.total,\n                .position = self.state.offset,\n                .viewport = self.state.viewport,\n                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n                .orientation = .vertical,\n            };\n            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// ScrollableList combines List behavior with virtual scrolling.\n/// Renders only visible items and integrates with ScrollState.\npub const ScrollableList = struct {\n    /// Items to display.\n    items: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Scroll state.\n    scroll: *ScrollState,\n\n    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection).\n    selected: ?usize = null,\n\n    /// Default style for non-selected items.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected item.\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Prefix shown before the selected item.\n    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n\n    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n\n    /// Scrollbar style.\n    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Update scroll state from items.\n    pub fn syncState(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        self.scroll.setTotal(self.items.len);\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Move selection up.\n    pub fn selectPrevious(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            if (sel > 0) {\n                self.selected = sel - 1;\n                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel - 1);\n            }\n        } else {\n            self.selected = 0;\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Move selection down.\n    pub fn selectNext(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            if (sel + 1 < self.items.len) {\n                self.selected = sel + 1;\n                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel + 1);\n            }\n        } else {\n            self.selected = 0;\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Select first item.\n    pub fn selectFirst(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        self.selected = 0;\n        self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n    }\n\n    /// Select last item.\n    pub fn selectLast(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        self.selected = self.items.len - 1;\n        self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.items.len - 1);\n    }\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input for navigation.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollableList, key: Key) bool {\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .up => {\n                self.selectPrevious();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .down => {\n                self.selectNext();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => {\n                self.selectFirst();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => {\n                self.selectLast();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_up => {\n                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n                    self.selected = sel -| page;\n                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_down => {\n                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n                    self.selected = @min(sel + page, self.items.len -| 1);\n                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Render the scrollable list.\n    pub fn render(self: ScrollableList, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Calculate content area (minus scrollbar if needed)\n        const needs_scrollbar = self.show_scrollbar and self.items.len > area.height;\n        const content_width = if (needs_scrollbar) area.width -| 1 else area.width;\n        const content_area = Rect.init(area.x, area.y, content_width, area.height);\n\n        if (content_area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, content_area.width));\n        const content_start = content_area.x +| symbol_len;\n        const text_width = content_area.width -| symbol_len;\n\n        // Get visible range\n        const range = self.scroll.visibleRange();\n\n        // Render visible items\n        var y = content_area.y;\n        var item_index = range.start;\n        while (item_index < range.end and y < content_area.bottom()) : ({\n            y += 1;\n            item_index += 1;\n        }) {\n            const item = self.items[item_index];\n            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n\n            if (is_selected) {\n                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n                const row_rect = Rect.init(content_area.x, y, content_area.width, 1);\n                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n\n                // Draw highlight symbol\n                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n                }\n\n                // Draw item text with highlight style\n                if (text_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n                }\n            } else {\n                // Draw item text with normal style\n                if (text_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n        if (needs_scrollbar) {\n            const sb_area = Rect.init(area.x +| content_width, area.y, 1, area.height);\n            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n                .total = self.items.len,\n                .position = self.scroll.offset,\n                .viewport = area.height,\n                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n                .orientation = .vertical,\n            };\n            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of items.\n    pub fn len(self: ScrollableList) usize {\n        return self.items.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if empty.\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: ScrollableList) bool {\n        return self.items.len == 0;\n    }\n};\n\n//      @memcpy(self.buffer[0..copy_len], content[0..copy_len]);\n    63→        self.len = copy_len;\n    64→        self.cursor = copy_len;\n    65→        self.anchor = copy_len;\n    66→   79→        if (self.max_len > 0) {\n    80→            return @min(self.max_len, self.buffer.len);\n    81→        }\n    82→        return self.buffer.len;\n    83→    }\n    84→\n    85→    // ========================================\n    86→    // Cursor Movement\n    87→    // ========================================\n    88→\n    89→    /// Move cursor left by one character.\n    90→    pub fn cursorLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n    91→        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n    92→            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n    93→        }\n    94→        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    95→    }\n    96→\n    97→    /// Move cursor right by one character.\n    98→    pub fn cursorRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n    99→        if (self.cursor < self.cursor != self.anchor;\n   136→    }\n   137→\n   138→    /// Get the selection range [start, end).\n   139→    pub fn selectionRange(self: TextInputState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n Replaces selection if active.\n   211→    pub fn insertBytes(self: *TextInputState, bytes: []const u8) void {\n   212→        // Delete selection first if present\n   213→        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n   214→            self.deleteSelection();\n   215→        }\n   216→\n   217→        const max = self.maxLength();\n   218→        const available = max -| self.len;\n   219→        const insert_len = @min(bytes.len, available);\n   220→        if (insert_len == 0) return;\n   221→\n   222→        // Make room by shifting content after cursor\n   223→        const   self.deleteSelection();\n   270→            return;\n   271→        }\n   272→\n   273→        if (self.cursor >= self.len) return;\n   274→\n   275→        const next =      self.buffer[next..self.len],\n   285→            );\n   286→        }\n   287→\n   288→        self.len -= delete_len;\n   289→    }\n   290→\n   291→    /// Delete word before cursor.\n   292→   298→        const target = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n   299→        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n   300→\n   301→        const delete_len = self.cursor - target;\n   302→ 313→        self.anchor = target;\n   314→    }\n   315→\n   316→    /// Delete word after cursor.\n   317→    pub fn deleteWordForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n   318→        if 324→        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n   325→\n   326→        const delete_len = target - self.cursor;\n   327→        const after = self.len - target;\n   328→        if (after > 0) {\n   329→            std.mem.copyForwards(\n   330→                u8,\n   331→                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n   332→                self.buffer[target..self.len],\n   333→            );\n   334→        }\n   335→\n   336→        self.len -= delete_len;\n   337→    }\n   338→\n   339→    /// Delete the current selection.\n   340→    fn deleteSelection(self: 362→    // ========================================\n   363→\n   364→    /// Copy selected text to provided buffer.\n   365→    /// Returns the copied text slice, or empty if no selection.\n   366→    pub fn copyTo(self: TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n   367→        if (!self.hasSelection()) return dest[0..0];\n   368→\n   369→        const selected = self.selectedText();\n   370→ true if the event was handled.\n   396→    pub fn handleKey(self: *TextInputState, key: Key) bool {\n   397→        const ctrl = key.modifiers.ctrl;\n   398→        const shift =   },\n   409→                        'w' => {\n   410→                            self.deleteWordBackward();\n   411→                            return true;\n   412→                        },\n   413→                        'u' => {\n   414→                            self.clear();\n   415→                            return true;\n   416→                        },\n   417→                        else => {},\n   418→                    }\n   419→                    return false;\n   420→                }\n   421→                // Regular character input\n   422→                self.insertChar(c);\n   423→                return true;\n   424→            },\n   425→            .left => {\n   426→                if (ctrl and shift) {\n   427→                    self.selectWordLeft();\n   428→                } else if (ctrl) {\n   429→                    self.cursorWordLeft();\n   430→                } else if (shift) {\n   431→                    self.selectLeft();\n   432→                } else {\n   433→                    self.cursorLeft();\n   434→                }\n   435→                return true;\n   436→            },\n   437→            .right => {\n   438→                if (ctrl and shift) {\n   439→                    self.selectWordRight();\n   440→                } else if (ctrl) {\n   441→ 446→                }\n   447→                return true;\n   448→            },\n   449→            .home => {\n   450→                if (shift) {\n   451→     }\n   463→                return true;\n   464→            },\n   465→            .backspace => {\n   466→                if (ctrl) {\n   467→                    self.deleteWordBackward();\n   468→                } else {\n   469→                    self.deleteBackward();\n   470→                }\n   471→                return true;\n   472→            },\n   473→            .delete => {\n   474→                if (ctrl) {\n   475→                    self.deleteWordForward();\n   476→                } else {\n   477→                    self.deleteForward();\n   478→                }\n   479→                return true;\n   480→            },\n   481→            else => {},\n   482→        }\n   483→        return false;\n   484→    }\n   485→\n   486→    // ========================================\n   487→    // UTF-8 Helpers\n   488→    // ========================================\n   489→\n   490→    /// Find the previous character boundary.\n   491→    fn prevCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   492→        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n   493→        var i = pos - 1;\n   494→        while (i > 0 and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n   495→            i -= 1;\n   496→        }\n   497→        return i;\n   498→    }\n   499→\n   500→    /// Find the next character boundary.\n   501→    fn nextCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   502→        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n   503→        var i = pos + 1;\n   504→        while (i < self.len and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n   505→            i += 1;\n   506→        }\n   507→        return i;\n   508→    }\n   509→\n   510→    /// Check if byte is a UTF-8 character start.\n   511→    fn isCharStart(byte: u8) bool {\n   512→        return (byte & 0xC0) != 0x80;\n   513→    }\n   514→\n   515→    /// Check if character is a word character.\n   516→    fn isWordChar(char: u8) bool {\n   517→        return std.ascii.isAlphanumeric(char) or char == '_';\n   518→    }\n   519→\n   520→    /// Find word boundary to the left.\n   521→    fn findWordBoundaryLeft(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   522→        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n   523→\n   524→        var i = pos;\n   525→\n   526→        // Skip any non-word characters immediately before cursor\n   527→        while (i > 0 and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n   528→            i -= 1;\n   529→        }\n   530→\n   531→        // Skip word characters\n   532→        while (i > 0 and isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n   533→            i -= 1;\n   534→        }\n   535→\n   536→        return i;\n   537→    }\n   538→\n   539→    /// Find word boundary to the right.\n   540→    fn findWordBoundaryRight(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   541→        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n   542→\n   543→        var i = pos;\n   544→\n   545→        // Skip word characters at cursor\n   546→        while (i < self.len and isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n   547→            i += 1;\n   548→        }\n   549→\n   550→        // Skip any non-word characters\n   551→        while (i < self.len and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n   552→            i += 1;\n   553→        }\n   554→\n   555→        return i;\n   556→    }\n   557→\n   558→    // ========================================\n   559→    // Display Helpers\n   560→    // ========================================\n   561→\n   562→    /// Calculate the display width of text up to a byte position.\n   563→    pub fn displayWidthTo(self: TextInputState, byte_pos: usize) usize {\n   564→        var width: usize = 0;\n   565→        var i: usize = 0;\n   566→        const content = self.buffer[0..@min(byte_pos, self.len)];\n   567→\n   568→        while (i < content.len) {\n   569→            const byte = content[i];\n   570→            if (byte < 0x80) {\n   571→                width += 1;\n   572→                i += 1;\n   573→            } else {\n   574→                const char_len = std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch {\n   575→                    i += 1;\n   576→                    continue;\n   577→                };\n   578→                if (i + char_len <= content.len) {\n   579→                    const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[i..][0..char_len]) catch {\n   580→                        i += 1;\n   581→                        continue;\n   582→                    };\n   583→                    // Rough approximation: CJK and emoji are double-width\n   584→                    if (codepoint >= 0x1100) {\n   585→                        width += 2;\n   586→                    } else {\n   587→                        width += 1;\n   588→                    }\n   589→                }\n   590→                i += char_len;\n   591→            }\n   592→        }\n   593→        return width;\n   594→    }\n   595→\n   596→    /// Update scroll offset to keep cursor visible.\n   597→    pub fn updateScrollOffset(self: *TextInputState, viewport_width: u16) void {\n   598→        if (viewport_width == 0) return;\n   599→\n   600→        const cursor_display_pos = self.displayWidthTo(self.cursor);\n   601→        const vw: usize = viewport_width;\n   602→\n   603→        if (cursor_display_pos < self.scroll_offset) {\n   604→            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos;\n   605→        } else if (cursor_display_pos >= self.scroll_offset + vw) {\n   606→            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos -| (vw -| 1);\n   607→        }\n   608→    }\n   609→};\n   610→\n   611→/// TextInput widget for rendering text input fields.\n   612→pub const TextInput = struct {\n   613→    /// Text input state.\n   614→    state: *TextInputState,\n   615→\n   616→    /// Default text style.\n   617→    style: Style = Style.empty,\n   618→\n   619→    /// Cursor style (when focused).\n   620→    cursor_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n   621→\n   622→    /// Selection highlight style.\n   623→    selection_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n   624→\n   625→    /// Placeholder text when empty.\n   626→    placeholder: []const u8 = \"\",\n   627→\n   628→    /// Placeholder style.\n   629→    placeholder_style: Style = Style.init().dim(),\n   630→\n   631→    /// Whether the input is focused (shows cursor).\n   632→    focused: bool = true,\n   633→\n   634→    /// Render the text input into the buffer.\n   635→    pub fn render(self: TextInput, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   636→        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   637→\n   638→        // Update scroll offset based on viewport\n   639→        self.state.updateScrollOffset(area.width);\n   640→\n   641→        // Fill background\n   642→        buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n   643→\n   644→        const content = self.state.text();\n   645→\n   646→        // Show placeholder if empty and not focused\n   647→        if (content.len == 0 and self.placeholder.len > 0 and !self.focused) {\n   648→            buf.setString(area.x, area.y, self.placeholder, self.placeholder_style);\n   649→            return;\n   650→        }\n   651→\n   652→        // Render visible text\n   653→        const selection = self.state.selectionRange();\n   654→        const scroll = self.state.scroll_offset;\n   655→\n   656→        var x: u16 = area.x;\n   657→        var byte_idx: usize = 0;\n   658→        var display_idx: usize = 0;\n   659→\n   660→        while (byte_idx < content.len and x < area.right()) {\n   661→            const byte = content[byte_idx];\n   662→            const char_len = if (byte < 0x80)\n   663→                @as(usize, 1)\n   664→            else\n   665→                std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch 1;\n   666→\n   667→            if (byte_idx + char_len > content.len) break;\n   668→\n   669→            const codepoint = if (byte < 0x80)\n   670→                @as(u21, byte)\n   671→            else\n   672→                std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[byte_idx..][0..char_len]) catch byte;\n   673→\n   674→            // Rough display width\n   675→            const char_width: usize = if (codepoint >= 0x1100) 2 else 1;\n   676→\n   677→            // Check if this character is visible\n   678→            if (display_idx + char_width > scroll) {\n   679→                // Determine style\n   680→                var char_style = self.style;\n   681→                const in_selection = self.state.hasSelection() and\n   682→                    byte_idx >= selection.start and byte_idx < selection.end;\n   683→\n   684→                if (in_selection) {\n   685→                    char_style = self.selection_style;\n   686→                }\n   687→\n   688→                // Draw cursor\n   689→                if (self.focused and byte_idx == self.state.cursor) {\n   690→                    char_style = self.cursor_style;\n   691→                }\n   692→\n   693→                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(codepoint, char_style));\n   694→                x += @intCast(@min(char_width, area.right() - x));\n   695→            }\n   696→\n   697→            display_idx += char_width;\n   698→            byte_idx += char_len;\n   699→        }\n   700→\n   701→        // Draw cursor at end if needed\n   702→        if (self.focused and self.state.cursor >= self.state.len) {\n   703→            if (x < area.right()) {\n   704→                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(' ', self.cursor_style));\n   705→            }\n   706→        }\n   707→    }\n   708→};\n   709→\n   710→// ============================================================\n   711→// SANITY TESTS - TextInputState basic functionality\n   712→//    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), state.cursor);\n  1057→\n  1058→    // Try to go before start\n  1059→    state.cursorHome();\n  1060→    state.cursorLeft();\n  1061→    try If different from cursor, text is selected.\n    /// Selection range is [min(anchor, cursor), max(anchor, cursor)).\n    anchor: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Horizontal scroll offset (for text wider than viewport).\n    scroll_offset: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Maximum allowed content length (0 = use buffer size).\n    max_len: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Create a new text input state with the given buffer.\n    pub fn init(backing_buffer: []u8) TextInputState {\n        return .{\n            .buffer = backing_buffer,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a text input state with initial content.\n    pub fn initWithContent(backing_buffer: []u8, initial: []const u8) TextInputState {\n        var state = init(backing_buffer);\n        state.setText(initial);\n        return state;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the current text content.\n    pub fn text(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n        return self.buffer[0..self.len];\n    }\n\n    /// Set the text content, replacing all existing content.\n    pub fn setText(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n        const max = self.maxLength();\n        const copy_len = @min(content.len, max);\n        @memcpy(self.buffer[0..copy_len], content[0..copy_len]);\n        self.len = copy_len;\n        self.cursor = copy_len;\n        self.anchor = copy_len;\n        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Clear all content.\n    pub fn clear(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.len = 0;\n        self.cursor = 0;\n        self.anchor = 0;\n        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Get maximum allowed length.\n    fn maxLength(self: TextInputState) usize {\n        if (self.max_len > 0) {\n            return @min(self.max_len, self.buffer.len);\n        }\n        return self.buffer.len;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Cursor Movement\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Move cursor left by one character.\n    pub fn cursorLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor right by one character.\n    pub fn cursorRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor to start of line.\n    pub fn cursorHome(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = 0;\n        self.anchor = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor to end of line.\n    pub fn cursorEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n        self.anchor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor left by one word.\n    pub fn cursorWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor right by one word.\n    pub fn cursorWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Selection\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Check if there is an active selection.\n    pub fn hasSelection(self: TextInputState) bool {\n        return self.cursor != self.anchor;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selection range [start, end).\n    pub fn selectionRange(self: TextInputState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n        return .{\n            .start = @min(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n            .end = @max(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selected text.\n    pub fn selectedText(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n        const range = self.selectionRange();\n        return self.buffer[range.start..range.end];\n    }\n\n    /// Clear selection (keep cursor position).\n    pub fn clearSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Select all text.\n    pub fn selectAll(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.anchor = 0;\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection left by one character.\n    pub fn selectLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection right by one character.\n    pub fn selectRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection to start of line.\n    pub fn selectToStart(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection to end of line.\n    pub fn selectToEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection left by one word.\n    pub fn selectWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection right by one word.\n    pub fn selectWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Editing\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Insert a character at cursor position.\n    /// Replaces selection if active.\n    pub fn insertChar(self: *TextInputState, char: u21) void {\n        var utf8_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n        const utf8_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(char, &utf8_buf) catch return;\n        self.insertBytes(utf8_buf[0..utf8_len]);\n    }\n\n    /// Insert text at cursor position.\n    /// Replaces selection if active.\n    pub fn insertBytes(self: *TextInputState, bytes: []const u8) void {\n        // Delete selection first if present\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n        }\n\n        const max = self.maxLength();\n        const available = max -| self.len;\n        const insert_len = @min(bytes.len, available);\n        if (insert_len == 0) return;\n\n        // Make room by shifting content after cursor\n        const after_cursor = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after_cursor > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyBackwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor + insert_len .. self.len + insert_len],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        // Insert new content\n        @memcpy(self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + insert_len], bytes[0..insert_len]);\n        self.len += insert_len;\n        self.cursor += insert_len;\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete character before cursor (backspace).\n    pub fn deleteBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (self.cursor == 0) return;\n\n        const prev = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        const delete_len = self.cursor - prev;\n\n        // Shift content after cursor\n        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[prev .. prev + after],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = prev;\n        self.anchor = prev;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete character at cursor (delete key).\n    pub fn deleteForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (self.cursor >= self.len) return;\n\n        const next = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        const delete_len = next - self.cursor;\n\n        // Shift content after deleted character\n        const after = self.len - next;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n                self.buffer[next..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete word before cursor.\n    pub fn deleteWordBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const target = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n\n        const delete_len = self.cursor - target;\n        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[target .. target + after],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = target;\n        self.anchor = target;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete word after cursor.\n    pub fn deleteWordForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const target = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n\n        const delete_len = target - self.cursor;\n        const after = self.len - target;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n                self.buffer[target..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete the current selection.\n    fn deleteSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (!self.hasSelection()) return;\n\n        const range = self.selectionRange();\n        const delete_len = range.end - range.start;\n        const after = self.len - range.end;\n\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[range.start .. range.start + after],\n                self.buffer[range.end..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = range.start;\n        self.anchor = range.start;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Clipboard Operations\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Copy selected text to provided buffer.\n    /// Returns the copied text slice, or empty if no selection.\n    pub fn copyTo(self: TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n        if (!self.hasSelection()) return dest[0..0];\n\n        const selected = self.selectedText();\n        const copy_len = @min(selected.len, dest.len);\n        @memcpy(dest[0..copy_len], selected[0..copy_len]);\n        return dest[0..copy_len];\n    }\n\n    /// Cut selected text to provided buffer.\n    /// Returns the cut text slice, or empty if no selection.\n    pub fn cutTo(self: *TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n        const copied = self.copyTo(dest);\n        if (copied.len > 0) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n        }\n        return copied;\n    }\n\n    /// Paste text from provided slice.\n    pub fn paste(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n        self.insertBytes(content);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Input Handling\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *TextInputState, key: Key) bool {\n        const ctrl = key.modifiers.ctrl;\n        const shift = key.modifiers.shift;\n\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .char => |c| {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    // Ctrl+key shortcuts\n                    switch (c) {\n                        'a' => {\n                            self.selectAll();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        'w' => {\n                            self.deleteWordBackward();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        'u' => {\n                            self.clear();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        else => {},\n                    }\n                    return false;\n                }\n                // Regular character input\n                self.insertChar(c);\n                return true;\n            },\n            .left => {\n                if (ctrl and shift) {\n                    self.selectWordLeft();\n                } else if (ctrl) {\n                    self.cursorWordLeft();\n                } else if (shift) {\n                    self.selectLeft();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorLeft();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .right => {\n                if (ctrl and shift) {\n                    self.selectWordRight();\n                } else if (ctrl) {\n                    self.cursorWordRight();\n                } else if (shift) {\n                    self.selectRight();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorRight();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => {\n                if (shift) {\n                    self.selectToStart();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorHome();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => {\n                if (shift) {\n                    self.selectToEnd();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorEnd();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .backspace => {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    self.deleteWordBackward();\n                } else {\n                    self.deleteBackward();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .delete => {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    self.deleteWordForward();\n                } else {\n                    self.deleteForward();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // UTF-8 Helpers\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Find the previous character boundary.\n    fn prevCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n        var i = pos - 1;\n        while (i > 0 and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Find the next character boundary.\n    fn nextCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n        var i = pos + 1;\n        while (i < self.len and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if byte is a UTF-8 character start.\n    fn isCharStart(byte: u8) bool {\n        return (byte & 0xC0) != 0x80;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if character is a word character.\n    fn isWordChar(char: u8) bool {\n        return std.ascii.isAlphanumeric(char) or char == '_';\n    }\n\n    /// Find word boundary to the left.\n    fn findWordBoundaryLeft(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n\n        var i = pos;\n\n        // Skip any non-word characters immediately before cursor\n        while (i > 0 and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n\n        // Skip word characters\n        while (i > 0 and isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Find word boundary to the right.\n    fn findWordBoundaryRight(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n\n        var i = pos;\n\n        // Skip word characters at cursor\n        while (i < self.len and isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        // Skip any non-word characters\n        while (i < self.len and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Display Helpers\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Calculate the display width of text up to a byte position.\n    pub fn displayWidthTo(self: TextInputState, byte_pos: usize) usize {\n        var width: usize = 0;\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        const content = self.buffer[0..@min(byte_pos, self.len)];\n\n        while (i < content.len) {\n            const byte = content[i];\n            if (byte < 0x80) {\n                width += 1;\n                i += 1;\n            } else {\n                const char_len = std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch {\n                    i += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                if (i + char_len <= content.len) {\n                    const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[i..][0..char_len]) catch {\n                        i += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    };\n                    // Rough approximation: CJK and emoji are double-width\n                    if (codepoint >= 0x1100) {\n                        width += 2;\n                    } else {\n                        width += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                i += char_len;\n            }\n        }\n        return width;\n    }\n\n    /// Update scroll offset to keep cursor visible.\n    pub fn updateScrollOffset(self: *TextInputState, viewport_width: u16) void {\n        if (viewport_width == 0) return;\n\n        const cursor_display_pos = self.displayWidthTo(self.cursor);\n        const vw: usize = viewport_width;\n\n        if (cursor_display_pos < self.scroll_offset) {\n            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos;\n        } else if (cursor_display_pos >= self.scroll_offset + vw) {\n            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos -| (vw -| 1);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// TextInput widget for rendering text input fields.\npub const TextInput = struct {\n    /// Text input state.\n    state: *TextInputState,\n\n    /// Default text style.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Cursor style (when focused).\n    cursor_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Selection highlight style.\n    selection_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Placeholder text when empty.\n    placeholder: []const u8 = \"\",\n\n    /// Placeholder style.\n    placeholder_style: Style = Style.init().dim(),\n\n    /// Whether the input is focused (shows cursor).\n    focused: bool = true,\n\n    /// Render the text input into the buffer.\n    pub fn render(self: TextInput, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Update scroll offset based on viewport\n        self.state.updateScrollOffset(area.width);\n\n        // Fill background\n        buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n\n        const content = self.state.text();\n\n        // Show placeholder if empty and not focused\n        if (content.len == 0 and self.placeholder.len > 0 and !self.focused) {\n            buf.setString(area.x, area.y, self.placeholder, self.placeholder_style);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Render visible text\n        const selection = self.state.selectionRange();\n        const scroll = self.state.scroll_offset;\n\n        var x: u16 = area.x;\n        var byte_idx: usize = 0;\n        var display_idx: usize = 0;\n\n        while (byte_idx < content.len and x < area.right()) {\n            const byte = content[byte_idx];\n            const char_len = if (byte < 0x80)\n                @as(usize, 1)\n            else\n                std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch 1;\n\n            if (byte_idx + char_len > content.len) break;\n\n            const codepoint = if (byte < 0x80)\n                @as(u21, byte)\n            else\n                std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[byte_idx..][0..char_len]) catch byte;\n\n            // Rough display width\n            const char_width: usize = if (codepoint >= 0x1100) 2 else 1;\n\n            // Check if this character is visible\n            if (display_idx + char_width > scroll) {\n                // Determine style\n                var char_style = self.style;\n                const in_selection = self.state.hasSelection() and\n                    byte_idx >= selection.start and byte_idx < selection.end;\n\n                if (in_selection) {\n                    char_style = self.selection_style;\n                }\n\n                // Draw cursor\n                if (self.focused and byte_idx == self.state.cursor) {\n                    char_style = self.cursor_style;\n                }\n\n                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(codepoint, char_style));\n                x += @intCast(@min(char_width, area.right() - x));\n            }\n\n            display_idx += char_width;\n            byte_idx += char_len;\n        }\n\n        // Draw cursor at end if needed\n        if (self.focused and self.state.cursor >= self.state.len) {\n            if (x < area.right()) {\n                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(' ', self.cursor_style));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n//
